[30;1m62 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m63 | [0m[35mPlease use HTML body instead if this causes problems. This is a problem [0m
[30;1m64 | [0m[35min smtplib itself and there is nothing to do with it at the moment. [0m

[30;1m5 | [0m[35m=======================[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35m[0m
